Perfect! Now I have a comprehensive understanding of the TTRSS architecture. Let me compile my findings:

## TTRSS Application Architecture - Comprehensive Analysis

I've thoroughly explored the Tiny Tiny RSS (TTRSS) application codebase. Here's a detailed breakdown of the architecture focusing on the key components you requested:

### Overall Structure

**Base Path:** `/Users/rd/devel/Capgemini/Capgemini_Internal/OSS_Migration/source-repos/ttrss-php/ttrss/`

The application is a PHP-based RSS feed aggregator built with an object-oriented architecture featuring a plugin system, multi-database support, and REST API.

---

### 1. DATABASE LAYER

**Entry Point:** `/include/db.php` (wrapper) and `/classes/db.php` (core)

**Architecture Pattern:** Singleton pattern with adapter design for multiple database backends

**Key Components:**

- **`Db` class** (`/classes/db.php`): Central singleton providing database abstraction
  - Dynamically selects adapter based on `DB_TYPE` configuration
  - Supports 4 database backends: PostgreSQL, MySQL, MySQLi, PDO
  - Interface: `IDb` defines contract for all adapters

- **Database Adapters:**
  - `/classes/db/pgsql.php` - PostgreSQL using `pg_*` functions
  - `/classes/db/mysql.php` - Legacy MySQL (deprecated functions)
  - `/classes/db/mysqli.php` - Modern MySQLi extension
  - `/classes/db/pdo.php` - PDO abstraction (universal)

**Configuration:** `/config.php-dist`
```php
DB_TYPE = "pgsql" or "mysql"
DB_HOST, DB_USER, DB_PASS, DB_NAME, DB_PORT
MYSQL_CHARSET = 'UTF8'
```

**Key Database Functions** (`/include/db.php`):
- `db_query()` - Execute queries
- `db_fetch_assoc()` / `db_fetch_result()` - Retrieve data
- `db_escape_string()` - Security escaping
- `db_num_rows()` / `db_affected_rows()` - Result inspection
- `db_last_error()` - Error handling

**Session Storage:** Sessions stored in `ttrss_sessions` table (custom handlers):
- `ttrss_open()`, `ttrss_read()`, `ttrss_write()`, `ttrss_close()`, `ttrss_destroy()`, `ttrss_gc()`

---

### 2. API STRUCTURE

**Entry Points:**
- `/api/index.php` - Primary REST API endpoint
- `/backend.php` - Fallback for public/compatibility calls
- `/classes/api.php` - Core API handler class

**API Design:**
- **Handler Pattern:** Routes through class methods (op parameter)
- **Authentication:** Session-based with API key support
- **Response Format:** JSON with seq, status, content wrapping
- **API Level:** Version 8 (defined in `API::API_LEVEL`)

**API Handler Class** (`/classes/api.php` extends `Handler`):
```php
Status codes:
- STATUS_OK = 0
- STATUS_ERR = 1

Key Methods:
- login() / logout() - Authentication
- isLoggedIn() - Session check
- getVersion() / getApiLevel() - Metadata
- getFeeds() / getCategories() - Feed structure
- getHeadlines() - Article retrieval
- getUnread() / getCounters() - Status data
- (40+ more RPC-style methods)
```

**Request/Response Structure:**
```json
Request: {"op": "method", "sid": "session_id", "param": "value"}
Response: {"seq": int, "status": 0/1, "content": {...}}
```

**Public API Calls** (before redirect to `/public.php`):
- `globalUpdateFeeds`, `rss`, `getUnread`, `getProfiles`, `share`, `fbexport`, `logout`, `pubsub`

---

### 3. PLUGIN SYSTEM

**Core Class:** `/classes/pluginhost.php` - Singleton managing plugin lifecycle

**Plugin Architecture:**
```php
- Plugin interface: extends Plugin base class
- API Version: 2 (defined in PluginHost::API_VERSION)
- Plugin types: SYSTEM (built-in), USER (installable)
```

**Hook System** (24 defined hooks):
```
HOOK_ARTICLE_BUTTON - Article actions
HOOK_ARTICLE_FILTER - Content filtering
HOOK_PREFS_TAB - Settings UI
HOOK_FEED_PARSED - RSS processing
HOOK_UPDATE_TASK - Feed updates
HOOK_AUTH_USER - Authentication
HOOK_HOTKEY_MAP - Keyboard shortcuts
HOOK_RENDER_ARTICLE - Display formatting
HOOK_SANITIZE - Content sanitization
HOOK_HOUSE_KEEPING - Maintenance tasks
(+ 14 more)
```

**Plugin Loading:**
- Location: `/plugins/[plugin_name]/init.php`
- Configuration: Loaded from `PLUGINS` config setting
- Auto-discovery: `load_all()` scans `/plugins/` directory
- System plugins: auto-loaded, cannot be disabled by users

**Plugin Interface:**
- `init($host)` - Initialize
- `about()` - Returns array with name, description, version, is_system flag
- `api_version()` - Must return 2+
- Hook registration: `register_hook(type, method)`

**Built-in System Plugins:**
- `auth_internal` - Database authentication
- `note` - Article annotations
- `updater` - Feed update daemon

---

### 4. AUTHENTICATION

**Method:** Internal database-based (primary), extensible via plugins

**Session Management** (`/include/sessions.php`):
- Custom session handler with database storage
- Session validation checks:
  - IP address validation (configurable: 0=off, 1=first 3 octets, 2=first 2, 3=full)
  - User agent hash matching
  - Password hash verification
  - Schema version consistency
  - Version static check

**Configuration:**
```php
SESSION_COOKIE_LIFETIME = 86400 (seconds)
SESSION_CHECK_ADDRESS = 1 (recommended)
SINGLE_USER_MODE = false (admin-only mode for single deployments)
AUTH_AUTO_CREATE = true (plugins can auto-create users)
AUTH_AUTO_LOGIN = true (auto-login on external auth)
```

**Authentication Flow:**
1. Login form (`/include/login_form.php`)
2. `authenticate_user($login, $password)` validates credentials
3. Session created with: `uid`, `pwd_hash`, `ip_address`, `user_agent`, `csrf_token`, `version`
4. For API: supports base64-encoded passwords

**CSRF Protection:**
- Token in session: `$_SESSION["csrf_token"]`
- Validated per handler via `csrf_ignore()` method

---

### 5. FEED PROCESSING ARCHITECTURE

**Core Feed Update** (`/include/rssfuncs.php`):

**Main Functions:**
- `update_daemon_common($limit, $from_http, $debug)` - Batch feed updater
- `update_feedbrowser_cache()` - Popular feeds cache
- `update_rss_feed($feed_id, $force, $no_cache)` - Single feed update

**Feed Update Process:**
1. Query feeds needing update (based on `update_interval` and `last_updated`)
2. Lock feeds with `last_update_started` timestamp (10-minute timeout)
3. Fetch RSS via HTTP (45-second timeout configurable)
4. Parse feed using SimplePie/FeedParser
5. Store articles in `ttrss_entries` (shared) and `ttrss_user_entries` (per-user)
6. Apply article filters via plugin hooks
7. Update counters and cache

**Feed Classes:**
- `/classes/feeds.php` - Handler for feed operations
- `/classes/feedparser.php` - RSS/Atom parsing
- `/classes/feeditem.php` - Feed entry abstraction
- `/classes/feedenclosure.php` - Media attachments

**Feed Data Model:**
```
ttrss_feeds - Feed subscriptions (per-user)
  Columns: id, owner_uid, title, link, feed_url, last_updated, 
           update_interval, last_update_started, error_msg, cache_images

ttrss_entries - Article content (shared across users)
  Columns: id, title, link, guid, updated, content, content_hash, 
           date_entered, date_updated

ttrss_user_entries - User-specific article state (per-user)
  Columns: int_id, ref_id, owner_uid, feed_id, unread, marked, 
           published, last_read, note, score
```

**Update Intervals & Daemon:**
- Configurable per-feed or default
- Daemon sleep interval: 120 seconds
- Login requirement: Only update feeds for users active in last 30 days
- Schema version check enforced

---

### 6. REQUEST ROUTING & HANDLERS

**Entry Points:**
1. `/index.php` - Web UI (HTML frontend)
2. `/backend.php` - JSON RPC backend
3. `/api/index.php` - REST API
4. `/public.php` - Public feeds (no auth required)

**Handler System** (`/classes/handler.php` base class):

**Hierarchy:**
```
Handler (base)
├── Backend (extends Handler)
├── API (extends Handler)
├── Handler_Protected (extends Handler)
│   ├── Feeds
│   ├── Article
│   └── Many preference handlers
└── Handler_Public (extends Handler)
```

**Handler Interface** (`IHandler`):
```php
- csrf_ignore($method) - Bypass CSRF check for specific methods
- before($method) - Pre-execution hook
- after() - Post-execution hook
```

**Routing Logic** (`/backend.php`):
```php
$op = $_REQUEST["op"]
$method = $_REQUEST["method"] or $_REQUEST["subop"]
// Instantiate handler class matching $op
// Call method if exists, else call index()
// Wrap JSON response with gzip if ENABLE_GZIP_OUTPUT
```

**Handler Methods Convention:**
- Camel case: `getFeeds()`, `editFeed()`, `getAllCounters()`
- Access via: `backend.php?op=feeds&method=getfeeds`
- Returns: JSON array for AJAX consumption

---

### 7. INITIALIZATION & BOOTSTRAP

**Bootstrap Sequence** (`/index.php`):
1. Check `config.php` existence (redirect to installer if missing)
2. Verify PHP 5.3+ requirement
3. Set include paths
4. Load: `autoload.php`, `sessions.php`, `functions.php`, `sanity_check.php`, `version.php`, `config.php`, `db-prefs.php`
5. Initialize gettext for i18n
6. Load Mobile_Detect library
7. Initialize plugins: `init_plugins()` -> `PluginHost::getInstance()->load()`
8. Route to digest/mobile plugins if applicable
9. Call `login_sequence()` - authentication check
10. Render HTML with JavaScript initialization

**JavaScript Libraries Used:**
- Dojo Toolkit (dijit widgets)
- Prototype.js + Scriptaculous
- Custom tt-rss.js, functions.js, viewfeed.js

---

### 8. KEY CONFIGURATION

**Essential Settings** (`/config.php-dist`):
```php
// Database
DB_TYPE = "pgsql"/"mysql"
DB_HOST, DB_USER, DB_PASS, DB_NAME, DB_PORT

// URLs & Paths
SELF_URL_PATH = "http://example.org/tt-rss/"
PHP_EXECUTABLE = "/usr/bin/php"
CACHE_DIR = "cache"
ICONS_DIR = "feed-icons"
LOCK_DIRECTORY = "lock"

// Performance
ENABLE_GZIP_OUTPUT = false
FEED_FETCH_TIMEOUT = 45

// Features
SINGLE_USER_MODE = false
SIMPLE_UPDATE_MODE = false
ENABLE_REGISTRATION = false
PUBSUBHUBBUB_ENABLED = false
SPHINX_ENABLED = false (fulltext search)

// Plugins
PLUGINS = "auth_internal, note, updater"

// Logging
LOG_DESTINATION = "sql" (or "syslog" or blank for PHP logging)
```

---

### 9. DATA FLOW SUMMARY

**Feed Update Flow:**
```
Daemon/HTTP → update_daemon_common() → Query feeds needing update
           → Lock with last_update_started
           → update_rss_feed() per feed
           → Fetch + Parse RSS
           → HOOK_FEED_FETCHED (plugin)
           → Store in ttrss_entries + ttrss_user_entries
           → HOOK_ARTICLE_FILTER (plugin)
           → Update counters via ccache_update()
           → Send digests if configured
```

**Article Display Flow:**
```
User Request (backend.php?op=feeds) → Feeds handler
                                     → Query ttrss_feeds + unread counts
                                     → Apply user preferences
                                     → Return JSON headlines
                                     → JavaScript renders in browser
```

**Authentication Flow:**
```
POST login form → login_sequence()
               → authenticate_user($login, $password)
               → Session created with CSRF token
               → Set secure cookie if HTTPS
               → Store in ttrss_sessions table
               → Validate on each request: IP, UA, version, pwd_hash
```

---

### 10. FILE ORGANIZATION

```
/include/
  ├── functions.php (53KB) - Core utility functions
  ├── functions2.php (68KB) - Additional utilities
  ├── rssfuncs.php (42KB) - Feed processing
  ├── sessions.php - Session handling
  ├── db.php - Database wrapper
  ├── db-prefs.php - User preferences
  ├── autoload.php - Class autoloading
  └── ... (15 other utilities)

/classes/
  ├── db.php - Singleton DB adapter
  ├── db/*.php - Database adapters (pgsql, mysql, mysqli, pdo)
  ├── api.php (22KB) - REST API handler
  ├── feeds.php (38KB) - Feed management
  ├── article.php (10KB) - Article operations
  ├── handler.php - Base handler
  ├── pluginhost.php (9KB) - Plugin management
  ├── plugin.php - Plugin base class
  ├── handler/ - Protected/Public handler variants
  ├── pref/ - Preference handlers (feeds, filters, users, etc.)
  ├── logger/ - Logging adapters
  └── ... (15+ utility classes)

/plugins/ - Plugin directory
  ├── auth_internal/
  ├── note/
  ├── updater/
  └── ... (user plugins)

/api/
  └── index.php - REST API entry point

/install/ - Installation wizard
/cache/ - Feed cache
/feed-icons/ - Cached favicons
/lock/ - Daemon lock files
```

---

### Key Architectural Strengths:

1. **Database Abstraction**: Supports multiple backends via adapter pattern
2. **Plugin System**: Extensible via 24 hooks without core modification
3. **Session Management**: Custom database-backed sessions with IP/UA validation
4. **API-First Design**: All operations available via REST API and internal RPC
5. **Multi-User Ready**: Per-user feeds, preferences, and subscriptions
6. **Daemon-Friendly**: Background feed updates with locking and throttling

This architecture enables TTRSS to be flexible, scalable, and maintainable for an RSS aggregation platform.

## Deployment Architecture Analysis

I've analyzed all 15 deployment and infrastructure files. Here's the complete architecture breakdown:

### 1. CONTAINERIZATION & ORCHESTRATION

**Dockerfile (Legacy - phusion/baseimage)**
- Base image: `phusion/baseimage:0.11` (minimal Ubuntu-based image with runit supervisor)
- Installs: nginx, php5-fpm, php5-cli, php5-gd, php5-mysql, htop, sudo
- Exposes port 80
- Uses runit service supervision via `/etc/runit/runsvdir/default`

**Dockerfile.local (Modern - PHP Apache)**
- Base image: `php:7.4-apache` (modern PHP with built-in Apache)
- Installs PHP extensions: gd (with freetype/jpeg), mysqli, pdo_mysql, zip
- Enables mod_rewrite for URL rewriting
- Document root: `/ttrss`
- Copies application code and runs `docker-entrypoint.sh`

**docker-compose.yaml (Production)**
- MySQL 5.5 database container (legacy)
- Application builds from main Dockerfile
- Port mapping: 80:80
- Volume: database data persistence
- Initializes schema from `ttrss/schema/ttrss_schema_mysql.sql`

**docker-compose.override.yml (Local Development)**
- MariaDB 10.3 database (modern replacement for MySQL)
- Service health checks enabled
- Depends on: database health check before app startup
- Environment variables for database connection and app config
- TT_REFRESH: 5 (feed update interval in minutes)

### 2. WEB SERVER CONFIGURATION (Nginx)

**nginx.conf**
- User: `www-data`
- Worker processes: 1
- Daemon mode: off (for container logging)
- Worker connections: 500
- Gzip compression enabled
- Logs to stdout for container capture
- Includes site configs from `/etc/nginx/sites-enabled/`

**sites-enabled/ttrss**
- Single server block listening on port 80
- Document root: `/ttrss`
- Default index files: index.html, index.htm, index.php
- FastCGI configuration for PHP files:
  - Unix socket: `/var/run/php5-fpm.sock`
  - Security: `try_files $uri = 404` prevents path traversal exploits
  - Uses standard fastcgi_params

### 3. PHP-FPM CONFIGURATION

**php5/fpm/pool.d/www.conf**
- Pool name: `www`
- User/Group: `www-data:www-data`
- Listen socket: `/var/run/php5-fpm.sock` with mode 0777
- Process manager: dynamic
- Child processes:
  - max_children: 5
  - start_servers: 2
  - min_spare_servers: 1
  - max_spare_servers: 3
- Working directory: `/`

### 4. ENTRYPOINT & INITIALIZATION

**docker-entrypoint.sh**
- Configurable via environment variables:
  - TT_DB_HOST (default: db)
  - TT_DB_NAME (default: ttrss)
  - TT_DB_USER (default: root)
  - TT_DB_PASS (default: ttrss)
  - TT_DOMAIN (default: localhost)
- Dynamically generates `/ttrss/config.php` with database credentials
- Creates cache subdirectories: images, upload, export, js
- Sets permissions: 755 for app, 777 for cache/lock/feed-icons
- Ownership: www-data:www-data

**TTRSS config.php (generated)**
- Database: MySQL with UTF8 charset
- Single user mode disabled (multi-user setup)
- Auto user creation and login enabled
- Feed update via PHP executable
- Plugins: auth_internal, note, updater
- Logging to SQL database
- No SMTP or Sphinx configured
- PUBSUBHUBBUB disabled
- Registration disabled
- Session lifetime: 86400 seconds (24 hours)

### 5. SERVICE SUPERVISION (runit)

**service/nginx/run**
- Minimal bash wrapper
- Executes: `nginx`

**service/php5-fpm/run**
- Minimal bash wrapper
- Executes: `php5-fpm -F` (foreground mode for supervision)

**service/update-feeds/run**
- Continuous background feed update process
- Configurable refresh interval (TT_REFRESH, default 5 minutes)
- Executes: `/ttrss/update.php --feeds --quiet`
- Runs as www-data user
- Sleeps between intervals

### 6. CI/CD PIPELINE (GitLab CI)

**.gitlab-ci.yml**
- Single job: `sonarqube-check`
- Runner: ubuntu
- Docker image: `sonarsource/sonar-scanner-cli:latest`
- Variables:
  - SONAR_USER_HOME: `.sonar` (caching)
  - GIT_DEPTH: 0 (fetch all branches)
- Caching: `.sonar/cache` per job
- Script: `sonar-scanner`
- Allow failure: true (doesn't block pipeline)
- Runs on all branches

**sonar-project.properties**
- Project key: PXMT
- Quality gate wait: enabled
- Minimal configuration (relies on sonar-scanner defaults)

### 7. SYSTEM CONFIGURATION

**etc/apt/sources.list**
- Ubuntu 14.04 Trusty repositories (old-releases)
- Includes: main, multiverse, restricted, universe components
- Covers: base, updates, security

**etc/rc.local** (Legacy startup script)
- Sources environment variables from `/etc/container_environment.sh`
- Removes default nginx site config
- Generates `/ttrss/config.php` with environment variables

### KEY ARCHITECTURAL CHARACTERISTICS

1. **Two Dockerfile strategies**: Legacy (runit supervision) vs Modern (Apache)
2. **Database options**: MySQL 5.5 (production) vs MariaDB 10.3 (dev)
3. **Service models**: runit process supervision (legacy) vs container foreground (modern)
4. **Configuration method**: Environment variables → Generated config.php at runtime
5. **Security features**: 
   - FastCGI path validation (`try_files $uri = 404`)
   - Socket-based PHP communication
   - Permission-restricted socket (0777)
6. **Background worker**: Continuous feed update daemon (every 5 minutes by default)
7. **Code quality**: SonarQube scanning in CI/CD pipeline
8. **Storage**: Database volume persistence, cache directories with relaxed permissions

## Comprehensive Analysis of TT-RSS Business Logic Layer

I've thoroughly analyzed the 32 PHP class files you specified. Here's my detailed findings:

### CLASS HIERARCHY & INHERITANCE PATTERNS

**Core Handler Hierarchy:**
- `Handler` (base class at `/classes/handler.php`)
  - Implements `IHandler` interface
  - Properties: `protected $dbh` (database handle), `protected $args`
  - Methods: `csrf_ignore()`, `before()`, `after()` lifecycle methods
  
- `Handler_Protected` extends `Handler`
  - Ensures authenticated sessions via `before()` method checking `$_SESSION['uid']`
  
- `Handler_Public` extends `Handler`
  - Allows unauthenticated access for public feeds/RSS generation

**Preference Classes (all extend Handler_Protected):**
- `Pref_Feeds` - Feed and category management
- `Pref_Filters` - Feed filter rules and actions
- `Pref_Labels` - User-defined labels/tags
- `Pref_Prefs` - User preferences and settings
- `Pref_Users` - Admin user management (access level check)
- `Pref_System` - System admin features (error logging)

**Business Logic Classes (all extend Handler_Protected):**
- `RPC` - Remote procedure calls for UI interactions
- `Article` - Article viewing, tagging, label operations
- `Feeds` - Feed display and management
- `Opml` - OPML import/export functionality
- `Dlg` - Dialog/popup rendering
- `PluginHandler` - Routes plugin method calls

**Feed Processing Classes:**
- `FeedParser` - XML/RSS/Atom parsing (DOM-based)
  - Detects feed type: `FEED_RDF`, `FEED_RSS`, `FEED_ATOM`
  - Uses DOMDocument and DOMXPath for parsing
  
- `FeedItem` (abstract base)
  - `FeedItem_Common` (abstract base for common extraction)
    - `FeedItem_Atom` - Atom entry extraction
    - `FeedItem_RSS` - RSS item extraction
  
- `FeedEnclosure` - Media enclosure data object

**Plugin Architecture:**
- `Plugin` - Base class for all plugins
  - Methods: `init()`, `about()`, `get_js()`, `get_prefs_js()`, `api_version()`
  
- `PluginHandler` - Routes requests to plugin methods via `catchall()`

**Database & Infrastructure:**
- `Logger` (singleton) - Error logging facade
  - `Logger_SQL` - Logs to database
  - `Logger_Syslog` - Logs to syslog
  
- `Db_Prefs` (singleton) - Preference caching and management
- `Db_Stmt` - Wrapper for prepared statement results
- `DbUpdater` - Schema versioning and migrations
- `ttrssMailer` extends PHPMailer - Email sending

**Authentication:**
- `Auth_Base` - Base authentication provider
- `IAuthModule` - Interface for auth modules

---

### DATABASE INTERACTION PATTERNS

**Query Patterns Observed:**

1. **Direct SQL with Manual Escaping:**
   ```
   $this->dbh->query("UPDATE ttrss_feeds SET title = '$title' WHERE id = '$id'");
   ```
   - Uses `$this->dbh->escape_string()` for input sanitization
   - No prepared statements (legacy approach)

2. **User Context Enforcement:**
   ```
   WHERE owner_uid = " . $_SESSION["uid"]
   ```
   - All user-specific queries filtered by `owner_uid` in session
   - Multi-tenancy through database schema

3. **Transaction Management:**
   ```
   $this->dbh->query("BEGIN");
   // ... operations ...
   $this->dbh->query("COMMIT");
   ```
   - Explicit transaction control for complex operations

4. **Preference Management Pattern:**
   - Cached in singleton `Db_Prefs`
   - Typed (bool, integer, string) conversion
   - Profile-based settings (multiple profiles per user)

5. **Result Iteration:**
   ```
   while ($line = $this->dbh->fetch_assoc($result)) { ... }
   ```
   - Standard array-based iteration pattern

---

### BUSINESS LOGIC ORGANIZATION

**1. Feed Management (Feeds class, ~1163 lines):**
- `format_headlines_list()` - Complex feed display logic
- `format_headline_subtoolbar()` - Article toolbar rendering
- `generate_dashboard_feed()` - Special feed generation
- `generate_error_feed()` - Error display
- `quickAddFeed()` - Subscribe to new feeds
- `feedBrowser()` - Feed discovery
- `search()` - Full-text search
- `catchupAll()` - Mark feeds as read

**2. Article Operations (Article class):**
- `view()` - Display article with prefetch support
- `setArticleTags()` - Tag assignment (with cache update)
- `assigntolabel()`/`removefromlabel()` - Label operations
- `setScore()` - Article scoring
- `editArticleTags()` - UI for tag editing
- `create_published_article()` (static) - Publish articles

**3. Article Marking Operations (RPC class):**
- `mark()` - Mark articles read/unread
- `delete()` - Delete articles
- `archive()` - Archive to separate table
- `unarchive()` - Restore archived articles
- `publ()` - Publish/share articles

**4. Preference Management:**
- `Pref_Prefs::saveconfig()` - Persist user preferences
- `Pref_Prefs::changepassword()` - Auth module delegation
- `Pref_Prefs::changeemail()` - User data updates
- `Db_Prefs` provides caching layer with type conversion

**5. Feed Filtering & Rules:**
- `Pref_Filters` manages filter creation/deletion
- `testFilter()` - Tests filter against recent articles
- Rules support: type matching, feed/category targets, actions
- Actions: assign labels, mark read, skip, etc.

**6. OPML Operations:**
- `opml_export()` - Full export with settings/filters/labels
- `opml_import()` - Bulk feed subscription
- Hierarchical category support

**7. Public Feed Generation (Handler_Public):**
- `generate_syndicated_feed()` - Outputs Atom/JSON format
- Supports published articles feed (-2)
- Respects `HTTP_IF_MODIFIED_SINCE` for caching
- Template-based rendering

---

### KEY ARCHITECTURAL PATTERNS

**1. Request Routing:**
- `Handler` base class uses `before()` for pre-processing
- Methods match HTTP `method` parameter (e.g., `?method=view`)
- `csrf_ignore()` determines CSRF protection per method
- `PluginHandler::catchall()` for dynamic plugin routing

**2. Access Control:**
- Session `$_SESSION["uid"]` for authentication
- Access level checks for admin functions (access_level >= 10)
- `Handler_Protected::before()` enforces login
- Row-level ownership via `owner_uid` database column

**3. Feed Parsing Strategy:**
- DOM-based (DOMDocument/DOMXPath) - requires full XML loading
- Namespace awareness (Atom03, Atom05, RSS, RDF)
- Graceful error handling with libxml error capture
- Encoding normalization for broken feeds

**4. Preference Abstraction:**
- Singleton `Db_Prefs` with in-memory cache
- Profile support (multiple settings per user)
- Type conversions (bool, integer, string)
- Used via global `get_pref()` and `set_pref()` functions

**5. Plugin System:**
- Plugin discovery via `PluginHost` (not shown but referenced)
- Hooks: `HOOK_QUERY_HEADLINES`, `HOOK_PREFS_TAB`, etc.
- Plugins can modify data via hook callbacks
- Method-based routing through `PluginHandler`

**6. Logging Strategy:**
- Adapter pattern: `Logger` delegates to `Logger_SQL` or `Logger_Syslog`
- Error handler registration captures PHP errors
- SQL logging includes user context for audit trail

---

### NOTABLE DESIGN DECISIONS

1. **No prepared statements** - SQL built with escaped strings
2. **No ORM** - Direct SQL queries with manual mapping
3. **Singleton patterns** - Logger, Db_Prefs for resource management
4. **Transaction usage** - Explicit for complex multi-step operations
5. **Cache layer** - Preferences cached in memory
6. **Template rendering** - MiniTemplator for feed generation
7. **Static methods** - `Article::create_published_article()` for general operations
8. **Direct session access** - Heavy reliance on `$_SESSION` throughout
9. **Plugin architecture** - Hooks before/after major operations
10. **Feed type detection** - Automatic based on XML root element

**File Locations:**
- Main business logic: `/classes/rpc.php`, `/classes/feeds.php`, `/classes/article.php`
- Preferences: `/classes/pref/*.php`
- Feed processing: `/classes/feedparser.php`, `/classes/feeditem/*.php`
- Infrastructure: `/classes/handler.php`, `/classes/plugin.php`, `/classes/logger/*.php`
- Database abstraction: `/classes/db/*.php`, `/classes/idb.php`
- Authentication: `/classes/auth/base.php`, `/classes/iauthmodule.php`

## Comprehensive Analysis of Tiny Tiny RSS (TTRSS) Codebase

### Directory Structure
**Base Path:** `/Users/rd/devel/Capgemini/Capgemini_Internal/OSS_Migration/source-repos/ttrss-php/ttrss/`

Key directories:
- `include/` - Core PHP utilities and business logic
- `classes/` - Object-oriented components (DB adapters, handlers, plugins)
- `js/` - Frontend JavaScript (Prototype/Dojo-based)
- `css/` - Styling
- `install/` - Installation scripts

---

### Database Architecture

**Schema Version:** 124 (SCHEMA_VERSION defined in functions.php)
**Database Support:** Both MySQL and PostgreSQL via adapter pattern

**Key Database Tables (inferred from code):**

1. **Core User Management**
   - `ttrss_users` - User accounts with `id, login, pwd_hash, access_level, last_login`
   - `ttrss_user_prefs` - User preferences with `owner_uid, pref_name, value, profile`
   - `ttrss_sessions` - Session storage with `id, data (base64-encoded), expire`

2. **Feed Management**
   - `ttrss_feeds` - Feed sources with `id, owner_uid, feed_url, title, site_url, auth_login, auth_pass, update_interval, last_updated, last_update_started, pubsub_state, cat_id`
   - `ttrss_feed_categories` - Feed categories with `id, owner_uid, title, parent_cat`
   - `ttrss_archived_feeds` - Archived feeds
   - `ttrss_feedbrowser_cache` - Cached feed directory
   - `ttrss_linked_feeds` - Linked/shared feeds

3. **Article/Entry Management**
   - `ttrss_entries` - Article content with `id, title, content, link, date_updated, date_entered`
   - `ttrss_user_entries` - User-specific article metadata with `id, owner_uid, feed_id, ref_id, int_id, unread, marked, published, score, label_cache, last_read`

4. **Labels/Tags**
   - `ttrss_labels2` - User labels with `id, owner_uid, caption, fg_color, bg_color`
   - `ttrss_user_labels2` - User-article label associations with `label_id, article_id`
   - `ttrss_tags` - Tags with `owner_uid, post_int_id, tag_name`

5. **Caching**
   - `ttrss_counters_cache` - Feed article count cache with `feed_id, owner_uid, value, updated`
   - `ttrss_cat_counters_cache` - Category count cache

6. **System**
   - `ttrss_version` - Schema version tracking
   - `ttrss_prefs` - Default preferences with `pref_name, def_value`
   - `ttrss_access_keys` - API access keys per user

---

### Authentication & Session Management

**Session System (include/sessions.php):**
- Custom session handler using database backend (`ttrss_sessions` table)
- Session name: `ttrss_sid` (with `_ssl` suffix for HTTPS)
- Session data stored as base64-encoded strings
- Session validation checks:
  - IP address matching (configurable via `SESSION_CHECK_ADDRESS`)
  - Password hash validation
  - User agent hash validation
  - Schema version consistency

**Authentication Flow (include/functions.php):**
1. `login_sequence()` - Main entry point for login handling
2. `authenticate_user($login, $password, $check_only)` - Core auth function
   - Supports plugin-based authentication via `PluginHost::HOOK_AUTH_USER`
   - Sets session: `uid, name, access_level, csrf_token, ip_address, user_agent, pwd_hash, version`
3. `validate_session()` - Session validation before each request
4. CSRF token generation using `uniqid(rand(), true)`

**Single User Mode:**
- Special mode for development/single-user installations
- Bypasses authentication, uses user ID 1

---

### Key Utility Functions

**Database Functions (include/db.php):**
- `db_query($query, $die_on_error)` - Execute query
- `db_fetch_assoc($result)` - Fetch associative row
- `db_num_rows($result)` - Get result set size
- `db_fetch_result($result, $row, $param)` - Get specific cell
- `db_escape_string($s, $strip_tags)` - SQL escaping
- `db_affected_rows($result)` - Rows affected by UPDATE/DELETE

**Preference Management (include/db-prefs.php):**
- `get_pref($pref_name, $user_id, $die_on_error)` - Get user preference
- `set_pref($pref_name, $value, $user_id, $strip_tags)` - Set user preference

**Cache Management (include/ccache.php):**
- `ccache_update($feed_id, $owner_uid, $is_cat)` - Update counter cache
- `ccache_find($feed_id, $owner_uid, $is_cat)` - Lookup cached count
- Supports both feed and category counters

**Label Management (include/labels.php):**
- `label_find_id()`, `label_create()`, `label_remove()`
- `get_article_labels()`, `label_update_cache()`
- Uses JSON encoding for label caching

**Feed Operations (include/rssfuncs.php):**
- `update_rss_feed($feed_id, $ignore_daemon, $no_cache)` - Main feed update logic
- `update_daemon_common()` - Batch update for daemon mode
- `update_feedbrowser_cache()` - Update directory cache

---

### Frontend-Backend Integration

**API Patterns:**
- **Backend Entry:** `backend.php` with `op` and `method` parameters
- **Public Entry:** `public.php` for login/registration
- **RPC Entry:** `backend.php?op=rpc&method=X` for data endpoints

**Frontend Initialization (js/functions.js):**
- Global variables: `init_params`, `loading_progress`, `sanity_check_done`
- CSRF token auto-injection via Ajax wrapper
- Exception reporting to server via `backend.php?op=rpc&method=log`

**Key JavaScript Files:**
1. **tt-rss.js** - Main application state and feed loading
   - `setActiveFeedId()`, `updateFeedList()`
   - `catchupAllFeeds()`, `viewCurrentFeed()`
   - Counter refresh via `request_counters()`

2. **viewfeed.js** - Article view logic
   - `viewfeed()` - Main feed content fetch
   - `headlines_callback2()` - Parse and render headlines
   - Implements infinite scroll via `loadMoreHeadlines()`

3. **feedlist.js** - Feed list management
   - `feedlist_init()` - Initialize feed tree
   - Hotkey binding and search

4. **functions.js** - Utility functions
   - Exception handling and error reporting
   - Parameter escaping/unescaping
   - Notification system
   - CSRF token injection

---

### Configuration & Constants

**Key Configuration Constants (functions.php):**
- `EXPECTED_CONFIG_VERSION` - 26
- `SCHEMA_VERSION` - 124
- `LABEL_BASE_INDEX` - -1024
- `PLUGIN_FEED_BASE_INDEX` - -128
- `FEED_FETCH_TIMEOUT`, `FILE_FETCH_TIMEOUT` - Network timeouts
- `DB_TYPE` - mysql or pgsql

**Configuration Files:**
- `config.php` - Main configuration (generated from `config.php-dist`)
- `sanity_config.php` - Auto-generated config validation
- Key defines: DB_HOST, DB_USER, DB_NAME, DB_PASS, SELF_URL_PATH, FEED_CRYPT_KEY

---

### Encryption & Security

**Feed Password Encryption (include/crypt.php):**
- Uses mcrypt with RIJNDAEL_128 in CBC mode
- Key: SHA256 hash of `FEED_CRYPT_KEY`
- Format: `base64(IV):base64(ciphertext)`

**Password Security:**
- `make_password()` - Generate random passwords (used for registration)
- Stored as hash (implementation via plugins)

**CSRF Protection:**
- Session-based token generation
- Auto-injected into AJAX requests
- Validated on backend requests

---

### Error Handling

**Error System (errors.php):**
- Server-side error definitions
- JavaScript error codes mapping
- Frontend exception dialog with:
  - Browser info collection
  - Stack trace capture
  - Error reporting to tt-rss.org (optional)

**Sanity Checks (include/sanity_check.php):**
- PHP version >= 5.3.0 required
- Required PHP extensions: curl/allow_url_fopen, JSON, MySQL/PostgreSQL, mbstring, hash, DOMDocument
- File permissions on cache/icon directories
- Configuration completeness validation

---

### Plugin Architecture

**Plugin System:**
- `classes/pluginhost.php` - Plugin loader and lifecycle management
- `classes/plugin.php` - Base plugin class
- Plugin hooks via `PluginHost::get_hooks(HOOK_NAME)`
- Load types: KIND_ALL, KIND_USER, KIND_SYSTEM
- Per-user enabled plugins stored in preference `_ENABLED_PLUGINS`

**Key Hooks:**
- `HOOK_AUTH_USER` - Authentication extension
- `HOOK_FETCH_FEED` - Feed fetching extension
- `HOOK_HOTKEY_INFO`, `HOOK_HOTKEY_MAP` - Keyboard shortcuts
- `HOOK_FEED_SET_ACTIVE`, `HOOK_FEED_LOADED` - Feed event hooks

---

### Special Features

**Digest System (include/digest.php):**
- Email digest of unread articles
- Scheduled per user with preferred time
- Supports automatic catchup of sent articles
- Uses template system (MiniTemplator)

**Preferences & Profiles:**
- Multi-profile support per user (schema >= 63)
- Preferences include: VIEW_MODE, UPDATE_INTERVAL, FEED_CATS, DIGEST settings, TIMEZONE
- Color scheme customization (USER_CSS_THEME)

**Icon Management:**
- Favicon extraction from feed sites
- Cached in `ICONS_DIR` with `ICONS_URL`
- Color palette generation for feed icons (include/colors.php)

---

### Critical File Paths

| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `include/autoload.php` | PSR-0 autoloader for classes |
| `include/functions.php` | Core utility functions (1000+ lines) |
| `include/functions2.php` | Feed/article query functions (1000+ lines) |

| `js/tt-rss.js` | Main app state and UI coordination |
| `js/viewfeed.js` | Article display and infinite scroll |
| `install/index.php` | Web-based installation wizard |

---

### Architectural Patterns

1. **Singleton Pattern** - Database instance (`Db::get()`)
2. **Adapter Pattern** - Database abstraction (MySQL/PostgreSQL)
3. **Hook Pattern** - Plugin extension system
4. **MVC-like** - Backend handlers separate from data layer
5. **Session-based State** - Stateful web application
6. **AJAX-driven UI** - Lightweight server-sent updates

## Complete Database Schema Summary

### Overview
The repository contains complete database schema definitions for Tiny Tiny RSS (TTRSS), a RSS feed reader. The schema is maintained in versioned migration files with support for both MySQL and PostgreSQL.

### Key Locations

**Complete Schema Files:**
- MySQL: `/Users/rd/devel/Capgemini/Capgemini_Internal/OSS_Migration/source-repos/ttrss-php/ttrss/schema/ttrss_schema_mysql.sql`
- PostgreSQL: `/Users/rd/devel/Capgemini/Capgemini_Internal/OSS_Migration/source-repos/ttrss-php/ttrss/schema/ttrss_schema_pgsql.sql`

**Schema Migration Framework:**
- `/Users/rd/devel/Capgemini/Capgemini_Internal/OSS_Migration/source-repos/ttrss-php/ttrss/classes/dbupdater.php` - Migration versioning system
- `/Users/rd/devel/Capgemini/Capgemini_Internal/OSS_Migration/source-repos/ttrss-php/ttrss/schema/versions/mysql/` - 124 incremental MySQL migration files (1.sql through 124.sql)
- `/Users/rd/devel/Capgemini/Capgemini_Internal/OSS_Migration/source-repos/ttrss-php/ttrss/schema/versions/pgsql/` - Parallel PostgreSQL migration files

### Complete Table Inventory (from mysql/124.sql)

**Core User Management:**
1. `ttrss_users` - User accounts with authentication, preferences, and profile data
2. `ttrss_sessions` - User session management
3. `ttrss_access_keys` - API access keys for users
4. `ttrss_user_prefs` - User preference overrides
5. `ttrss_settings_profiles` - Named preference profiles per user

**Feed Management:**
6. `ttrss_feeds` - RSS feed definitions with metadata
7. `ttrss_feed_categories` - Feed organization/categorization
8. `ttrss_archived_feeds` - Historical feed records
9. `ttrss_scheduled_updates` - Feed update scheduling

**Content/Articles:**
10. `ttrss_entries` - Individual RSS articles/entries
11. `ttrss_user_entries` - User-specific article metadata (read status, marks, scores)
12. `ttrss_entry_comments` - Comments on articles

**Tagging & Labeling:**
13. `ttrss_tags` - Article tags
14. `ttrss_labels2` - User labels (with colors)
15. `ttrss_user_labels2` - Label-to-article mappings

**Filtering:**
16. `ttrss_filters2` - Advanced filter rules
17. `ttrss_filters2_rules` - Individual filter rule conditions
18. `ttrss_filters2_actions` - Filter action definitions
19. `ttrss_filter_types` - Filter type reference (title, content, link, date, author, tags)
20. `ttrss_filter_actions` - Filter action reference (delete, mark read, star, tag, publish, score, label)
21. `ttrss_filters` - Deprecated legacy filters table

**Media & Enclosures:**
22. `ttrss_enclosures` - Podcast/media attachments to articles

**Caching & Performance:**
23. `ttrss_counters_cache` - Feed unread count cache
24. `ttrss_cat_counters_cache` - Category unread count cache
25. `ttrss_feedbrowser_cache` - Public feed directory cache

**Preferences & Configuration:**
26. `ttrss_prefs` - System preference definitions
27. `ttrss_prefs_types` - Preference data type reference (bool, string, integer)
28. `ttrss_prefs_sections` - Preference section grouping
29. `ttrss_themes` - UI theme definitions
30. `ttrss_version` - Schema version tracking

**Plugin System:**
31. `ttrss_plugin_storage` - Plugin persistent storage

**Federation/Linking:**
32. `ttrss_linked_instances` - Remote TTRSS instance connections
33. `ttrss_linked_feeds` - Feeds from linked instances

**Error Logging:**
34. `ttrss_error_log` - Application error tracking
35. `ttrss_labels` - Deprecated legacy labels table

### Key Relationships & Foreign Keys

**User Hierarchy:**
- `ttrss_feeds.owner_uid` → `ttrss_users.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_feed_categories.owner_uid` → `ttrss_users.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_user_entries.owner_uid` → `ttrss_users.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_tags.owner_uid` → `ttrss_users.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_labels2.owner_uid` → `ttrss_users.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_filters2.owner_uid` → `ttrss_users.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_user_prefs.owner_uid` → `ttrss_users.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_settings_profiles.owner_uid` → `ttrss_users.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_access_keys.owner_uid` → `ttrss_users.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_plugin_storage.owner_uid` → `ttrss_users.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)

**Feed Structure:**
- `ttrss_feeds.cat_id` → `ttrss_feed_categories.id` (ON DELETE SET NULL)
- `ttrss_feeds.parent_feed` → `ttrss_feeds.id` (ON DELETE SET NULL, for feed subscriptions)
- `ttrss_feed_categories.parent_cat` → `ttrss_feed_categories.id` (ON DELETE SET NULL, for category nesting)

**Article Content:**
- `ttrss_user_entries.ref_id` → `ttrss_entries.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_user_entries.feed_id` → `ttrss_feeds.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_user_entries.orig_feed_id` → `ttrss_archived_feeds.id` (ON DELETE SET NULL)
- `ttrss_entry_comments.ref_id` → `ttrss_entries.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_entry_comments.owner_uid` → `ttrss_users.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_tags.post_int_id` → `ttrss_user_entries.int_id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_enclosures.post_id` → `ttrss_entries.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_user_labels2.label_id` → `ttrss_labels2.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_user_labels2.article_id` → `ttrss_entries.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)

**Filtering:**
- `ttrss_filters2_rules.filter_id` → `ttrss_filters2.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_filters2_rules.filter_type` → `ttrss_filter_types.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_filters2_rules.feed_id` → `ttrss_feeds.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_filters2_rules.cat_id` → `ttrss_feed_categories.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_filters2_actions.filter_id` → `ttrss_filters2.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_filters2_actions.action_id` → `ttrss_filter_actions.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)

**Preferences:**
- `ttrss_prefs.type_id` → `ttrss_prefs_types.id`
- `ttrss_prefs.section_id` → `ttrss_prefs_sections.id`
- `ttrss_user_prefs.pref_name` → `ttrss_prefs.pref_name` (ON DELETE CASCADE)
- `ttrss_user_prefs.profile` → `ttrss_settings_profiles.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)

**Federation:**
- `ttrss_linked_feeds.instance_id` → `ttrss_linked_instances.id` (ON DELETE CASCADE)

**Error Logging:**
- `ttrss_error_log.owner_uid` → `ttrss_users.id` (ON DELETE SET NULL)

### Database Migration System

The DbUpdater class (`dbupdater.php`) implements a versioning system:
- Tracks current schema version in `ttrss_version.schema_version`
- Applies incremental SQL migrations sequentially
- Current schema version: **124**
- Migrations span from version 1 through 124 (MySQL and PostgreSQL parallels)
- Each migration is wrapped in BEGIN/COMMIT for transaction safety

### Seed Data

The schema includes default seed data:
1. Admin user: login='admin', password hash='SHA1:5baa61e4c9b93f3f0682250b6cf8331b7ee68fd8'
2. Default feeds (2 TTRSS official feeds)
3. Filter types reference (7 types: title, content, both, link, date, author, tag)
4. Filter actions reference (8 actions: filter, catchup, mark, tag, publish, score, label, stop)
5. Preference types reference (3 types: bool, string, integer)
6. Preference sections (4 sections)
7. 40+ system default preferences with various configurations

### Special Features

1. **Hierarchical Categories:** Feed categories support parent-child relationships
2. **Feed Subscriptions:** Parent feed references enable subscription grouping
3. **User Entries Bridge:** `ttrss_user_entries` links articles to feeds and users with per-user metadata
4. **Plugin Storage:** Dynamic storage table for plugins
5. **Access Keys:** API authentication separate from user passwords
6. **Linked Instances:** Federation support for connecting to other TTRSS instances
7. **Settings Profiles:** Multiple preference profiles per user
8. **Tag Caching:** Performance optimization with cached tag/label lists per article

### File Summary

- **2 Complete schema definitions** (MySQL + PostgreSQL)
- **248 total migration files** (124 MySQL + 124 PostgreSQL versions)
- **1 Migration framework file** (DbUpdater class)
- **Complete schema with 35 tables**
- **Extensive foreign key constraints** with cascading deletes for data integrity

### 7. PLUGIN HOOK CALL SITES

**Primary Hook Sites:**
```
index.php:36-42        → PluginHost::getInstance()->get_plugin("digest"|"mobile")
index.php:80           → PluginHost::getInstance()->get_plugins() [loop]
index.php:110-113      → Plugin->get_css(), Plugin->get_js()
index.php:213          → PluginHost::getInstance()->get_hooks(HOOK_TOOLBAR_BUTTON)
index.php:252          → PluginHost::getInstance()->get_hooks(HOOK_ACTION_ITEM)
update.php:39, 89      → PluginHost::getInstance()->get_commands()
update.php:161, 190    → PluginHost::getInstance()->run_hooks(HOOK_UPDATE_TASK, "hook_update_task", $op)
update.php:355         → PluginHost::getInstance()->run_commands($options)
backend.php:116        → PluginHost::getInstance()->lookup_handler($op, $method)
public.php:40          → PluginHost::getInstance()->lookup_handler("public", $method)
```

**Hook Registration Flow:**
1. `init_plugins()` loads plugin classes
2. Each plugin's `init($host)` method registers hooks via `$host->register_hook()`
3. At runtime, `PluginHost::getInstance()->run_hooks()` invokes registered hook handlers
4. Plugins can override handlers via `lookup_handler()`

---

### 8. DATABASE INTERACTION POINTS

**Legacy db_* Functions** (all delegate to Db::get()):
- **Query Execution**: `db_query()` - used in 100+ locations
- **Data Fetching**: `db_fetch_assoc()`, `db_fetch_result()` - used in 100+ locations
- **Utility**: `db_num_rows()`, `db_affected_rows()`, `db_last_error()`, `db_escape_string()`, `db_quote()`

**Object-Oriented Access** ($this->dbh->):
- Used in handler classes when they need database access
- `$this->dbh = Db::get()` in Handler, PluginHost constructors
- Methods called: `query()`, `fetch_assoc()`, `fetch_result()`, `escape_string()`, `num_rows()`, `affected_rows()`

**Adapter-Based Database Support:**
- DB_TYPE determines which adapter is instantiated (mysql, mysqli, pgsql, pdo)
- Each adapter implements the full IDb interface
- Db class proxies all calls to the selected adapter

---

### 9. CRITICAL INTER-FILE FUNCTION CALLS

**Main Request Flow:**
```
index.php/backend.php/api/index.php
  → require autoload.php (enables class autoloading)
  → require functions.php (core utilities)
  → call init_plugins() [functions.php]
    → PluginHost::getInstance()
    → load plugin classes
    → call each plugin->init($host)
  → (if user logged in) load_user_plugins($uid) [functions.php]
  → authenticate_user() or login_sequence() [functions.php]
  → Handler instantiation: new $op($_REQUEST) or lookup_handler() via PluginHost
  → Handler->before() → Handler->$method() → Handler->after()
```

**Database Flow:**
```
Any code → db_query($sql)
  → Db::get()->query($sql) [singleton]
  → $adapter->query($sql)
    → Db_Mysqli/Db_Mysql/Db_Pgsql/Db_PDO->query($sql)
    → Returns result resource/object
```

**Feed Update Flow:**
```
update_daemon2.php
  → require rssfuncs.php
  → call purge_orphans()
  → PluginHost::getInstance()->run_hooks(HOOK_UPDATE_TASK)
  → For each feed: call update_rss_feed($feed_id)
    → fetch_file_contents()
    → FeedParser->parse()
    → FeedItem_Atom/FeedItem_RSS processing
    → db_query() for database inserts/updates
```

Perfect! Now I have all the information I need. Let me create a comprehensive analysis document:

## COMPREHENSIVE FRONTEND-BACKEND INTEGRATION ANALYSIS: TT-RSS

### ARCHITECTURE OVERVIEW

TT-RSS uses a **classic RPC (Remote Procedure Call) architecture** with:
- **Frontend**: Prototype.js + Dojo Toolkit (dijit widgets, dojo.data stores, Trees)
- **Backend**: PHP handler classes following a strict pattern
- **Communication**: Ajax.Request with JSON responses
- **Data flow**: All interaction goes through `backend.php` which dispatches to handler classes

---

### CORE ROUTING MECHANISM (backend.php)

**File**: `/Users/rd/devel/Capgemini/Capgemini_Internal/OSS_Migration/source-repos/ttrss-php/ttrss/backend.php`

```php
$op = $_REQUEST["op"];                          // Operation/Handler class name
$method = $_REQUEST['subop'] ? $_REQUEST['subop'] : $_REQUEST["method"]; // Handler method
```

**Dispatch Logic**:
1. Op is converted to class name: `op=pref-feeds` → `class Pref_Feeds`
2. Method name is lowercased
3. Handler class must implement `IHandler` interface
4. Handler::$method() is called
5. Output is always JSON (`Content-Type: text/json`)

---

### HANDLER CLASS HIERARCHY

**Base Interface**: `IHandler`
```php
interface IHandler {
    function csrf_ignore($method);  // Which methods skip CSRF validation
    function before($method);        // Pre-processing
    function after();                // Post-processing
}
```

**Base Class**: `Handler implements IHandler`
- Protected properties: `$dbh` (database), `$args` ($_REQUEST)
- Default: csrf_ignore returns true, before/after return true

**Handler Inheritance Chain**:
```
Handler (base)
├── Handler_Protected (requires authentication)
│   ├── RPC (op=rpc) - State-changing operations
│   ├── Feeds (op=feeds) - Feed viewing and metadata
│   ├── Article (op=article) - Article operations
│   ├── Pref_Feeds (op=pref-feeds) - Feed preferences
│   ├── Pref_Filters (op=pref-filters) - Filter management
│   ├── Pref_Labels (op=pref-labels) - Label management
│   ├── Pref_Users (op=pref-users) - User management
│   ├── Pref_Prefs (op=pref-prefs) - Global preferences
│   ├── Pref_System (op=pref-system) - System settings
│   ├── Dlg (op=dlg) - Dialog content
│   ├── Opml (op=opml) - OPML import/export
│   └── PluginHandler (op=plugin_*) - Plugin operations
│
├── Handler_Public (public endpoints)
└── Backend (op=backend) - System operations
└── API (op=api) - API endpoints
```

---

### KEY RPC ENDPOINTS (op=rpc)

**File**: `/Users/rd/devel/Capgemini/Capgemini_Internal/OSS_Migration/source-repos/ttrss-php/ttrss/classes/rpc.php`

| Method | Purpose | Input | Output |
|--------|---------|-------|--------|
| `sanityCheck` | Initial connection check | hasAudio, hasMp3, clientTzOffset, hasSandbox | JSON with error/message |
| `mark` | Toggle article starred status | id, mark (0/1) | UPDATE_COUNTERS message |
| `publ` | Toggle article published status | id, pub (0/1) | UPDATE_COUNTERS message |
| `delete` | Delete articles | ids (comma-separated) | UPDATE_COUNTERS message |
| `archive` | Archive articles | ids | UPDATE_COUNTERS message |
| `getAllCounters` | Get unread counts | seq, last_article_id | counters array |
| `catchupSelected` | Mark selected read | ids | UPDATE_COUNTERS message |
| `markSelected` | Star selected articles | ids | UPDATE_COUNTERS message |
| `publishSelected` | Mark selected published | ids | UPDATE_COUNTERS message |
| `catchupFeed` | Mark entire feed read | feed_id, is_cat, mode | UPDATE_COUNTERS message |
| `setpref` | Save user preference | key, value | param/value JSON |
| `setpanelmode` | Save panel layout | wide (0/1) | (silent) |
| `setprofile` | Switch settings profile | id | (silent) |
| `addprofile` | Create new profile | title | (silent) |
| `remprofiles` | Delete profiles | ids | (silent) |
| `addfeed` | Subscribe to feed | feed, cat, login, pass | result JSON |
| `quickAddCat` | Create feed category | cat | (silent) |

### FEEDS HANDLER (op=feeds)

| Method | Purpose | Input | Output |
|--------|---------|-------|--------|
| `view` | Load headlines for feed | feed, view_mode, order_by, skip (offset), m (method) | JSON with headlines content/toolbar/metadata |
| `catchupAll` | Mark all feeds read | (none) | (redirects or silent) |
| `search` | Search articles | q, smode | Search results in feed view format |
| `quickAddFeed` | Open feed subscription dialog | (none) | HTML for dialog |
| `feedBrowser` | Browse available feeds | search, limit | HTML table of feeds |

**Response Structure** (view method):
```javascript
{
  headlines: {
    id: feed_id,
    is_cat: boolean,
    content: "<div id='RROW-123'>...</div>...",  // Server-rendered HTML
    toolbar: "<div>...</div>"                      // Server-rendered toolbar
  },
  'headlines-info': {
    count: 30,
    vgroup_last_feed: null,
    disable_cache: false
  },
  counters: [ {id, kind, counter, error, updated, has_img, auxcounter}, ... ],
  'runtime-info': { daemon_is_running, etc }
}
```

### PREFERENCES HANDLERS

#### Pref_Feeds (op=pref-feeds)
- `getfeedtree()` - Returns JSON tree for dojo.data.ItemFileWriteStore
- `makefeedtree()` - Builds hierarchical feed/category structure
- `editfeed(id)` - Open feed edit dialog
- `editfeeds(ids)` - Batch edit dialog
- `editSave()` - Save single feed
- `batchEditSave()` - Save batch edits
- `remove(ids)` - Unsubscribe from feeds
- `addCat(cat)` - Create feed category
- `removeCat(ids)` - Delete categories
- `rescore(ids)` - Recalculate article scores
- `feedsWithErrors()` - List feeds with errors

#### Pref_Filters (op=pref-filters)
- Manage article filtering rules
- `newfilter()` - Create filter UI
- `printrulename(rule)` - Get rule description
- `printactionname(action)` - Get action description

#### Pref_Labels (op=pref-labels)
- Manage article labels/tags
- `edit(id)` - Open label editor
- `colorset()` - Set label color

#### Pref_Users (op=pref-users)
- Manage system users (admin only)

#### Pref_Prefs (op=pref-prefs)
- Global and user preferences
- `editPrefProfiles()` - Manage settings profiles

### JAVASCRIPT AJAX PATTERNS

**Pattern 1: Basic RPC Call**
```javascript
new Ajax.Request("backend.php", {
    parameters: "?op=rpc&method=mark&id=" + id + "&mark=1",
    onComplete: function(transport) {
        handle_rpc_json(transport);
    }
});
```

**Pattern 2: Dialog/Content Loading**
```javascript
dialog = new dijit.Dialog({
    id: "userEditDlg",
    title: __("User Editor"),
    href: "backend.php?op=pref-users&method=edit&id=" + id
});
dialog.show();
```

**Pattern 3: Tree Data Loading**
```javascript
var store = new dojo.data.ItemFileWriteStore({
    url: "backend.php?op=pref_feeds&method=getfeedtree&mode=2"
});
var treeModel = new fox.FeedStoreModel({
    store: store,
    query: { type: "feed" },  // Filter by type
    rootId: "root",
    childrenAttrs: ["items"]
});
```

**Pattern 4: Post Data Form**
```javascript
dojo.xhrPost({
    url: "backend.php",
    content: {
        op: "pref-feeds",
        method: "editSave",
        id: feed_id,
        title: title,
        feed_url: url
    }
});
```

### DOM MANIPULATION LIBRARIES

**Prototype.js**:
- `$()` - Element selection by ID
- `$(element).addClassName() / removeClassName()`
- `$(element).setStyle() / getStyle()`
- `Element.show() / Element.hide() / Element.visible()`
- String extensions: `.toQueryParams(), .toQueryString()`

**Dojo Toolkit**:
- `dijit.byId(id)` - Get widget by ID
- `dijit.Dialog` - Modal dialogs
- `dijit.form.*` - Form widgets (TextBox, CheckBox, Select, Button)
- `dojo.data.ItemFileWriteStore` - Client-side data store
- `dojo.xhrPost / dojo.xhrGet` - XHR requests
- `dojo.connect / dojo.disconnect` - Event binding
- `dojo.html.set()` - Set HTML content

---

### RESPONSE DATA FLOW

**Typical Article View Flow**:

1. **Frontend** calls: `new Ajax.Request("backend.php", parameters: "?op=feeds&method=view&feed=5")`

2. **Backend** Feeds::view() executes:
   - Queries articles from database
   - Calls format_headlines_list() which renders HTML rows: `<div id='RROW-123'>...</div>`
   - Returns JSON with 'headlines']['content'] = server-rendered HTML

3. **Frontend** headlines_callback2() processes:
   - Parses JSON response
   - Sets `dijit.byId("headlines-frame").attr('content', reply['headlines']['content'])`
   - Calls dojo.parser.parse() to initialize any embedded Dojo widgets
   - Updates counters display

4. **DOM Updates**:
   - Article rows DOM elements are created server-side, inserted client-side
   - Clicking article calls view(id) → Article::view()
   - Returns JSON with article content
   - Frontend inserts into content pane

---

### CSRF PROTECTION

**Pattern**: CSRF token in all AJAX requests

```javascript
// In functions.js:
Ajax.Base.prototype.initialize = Ajax.Base.prototype.initialize.wrap(
    function(callOriginal, options) {
        if (getInitParam("csrf_token") != undefined) {
            options.parameters["csrf_token"] = getInitParam("csrf_token");
        }
        return callOriginal(options);
    }
);

// In backend.php:
$csrf_token = $_REQUEST['csrf_token'];
if (!validate_csrf($csrf_token) && !$handler->csrf_ignore($method)) {
    // Error 6
}
```

Some methods are CSRF-ignored for public access:
- RPC: sanitycheck, completelabels
- Feeds: index, feedbrowser, quickaddfeed, search
- Article: redirect, editarticletags

---

### WIDGET/FORM PATTERNS

**Dialog with Form**:
```javascript
dialog = new dijit.Dialog({
    id: "filterEditDlg",
    href: "backend.php?op=pref-filters&method=edit&id=" + id,
    execute: function() {
        if (this.validate()) {
            new Ajax.Request("backend.php", {
                parameters: dojo.formToQuery("filter_edit_form"),
                onComplete: function(transport) {
                    dijit.byId('filterEditDlg').hide();
                    updateFeedList();
                }
            });
        }
    }
});
```

**Tree Widget**:
```javascript
var store = new dojo.data.ItemFileWriteStore({
    url: "backend.php?op=pref_feeds&method=getfeedtree&mode=2"
});
var tree = new fox.FeedTree({
    model: new fox.FeedStoreModel({store: store}),
    onClick: function(item) {
        // Item properties: id, name, unread, error, updated, has_img
    }
});
```

---

### SERVER-SIDE HTML RENDERING

The backend renders **most HTML server-side** in two contexts:

**1. Headlines List** (Feeds::format_headlines_list):
```php
$content .= "<div id='RROW-$id' class='$classes'>";
$content .= "<div class='hlContent'>";
$content .= "<a href='#'>" . htmlspecialchars($title) . "</a>";
$content .= "<span class='hlUpdated'>$updated</span>";
// ... more HTML
$content .= "</div>";

return array('content' => $content, 'toolbar' => $toolbar_html);
```

**2. Dialog Content** (various pref handlers):
```php
// In prefs.js callback:
dijit.byId('feedConfigTab').attr('content', transport.responseText);
// transport.responseText is HTML with dojoType attributes:
// <input dojoType="dijit.form.TextBox" name="feed_url">
// dojo.parser.parse() initializes these
```

---

### COMPLETE AJAX CALL MAPPING

| Frontend Call | Backend Handler | Method | Purpose |
|---|---|---|---|
| `new Ajax.Request("backend.php", {parameters: "?op=rpc&method=sanityCheck..."})` | RPC | sanityCheck | Verify backend connectivity |
| `viewfeed(5, '', false)` | Feeds | view | Load headlines for feed 5 |
| `view(123)` | Article | view | Load article 123 content |
| `editFeed(5)` | Pref_Feeds | editfeed | Open feed editor |
| `editArticleTags(123)` | Article | editArticleTags | Open tag editor |
| `catchupFeed(5, false)` | RPC | catchupFeed | Mark feed 5 as read |
| `updateFeedList()` | Pref_Feeds | index | Reload feed list |
| `request_counters()` | RPC | getAllCounters | Get unread counts |
| `editFilter(7)` | Pref_Filters | edit | Open filter editor |
| `addLabel()` | Pref_Labels | edit | Create new label |
| `quickAddFeed()` | Feeds | quickAddFeed | Show feed subscription form |

---

### SUMMARY: THE EXACT FRONTEND-BACKEND CONTRACT

1. **All requests** go through `backend.php` with `op` and `method` parameters
2. **Classes** are named `Op` (underscores from hyphens) and must implement `IHandler`
3. **Methods** are public, lowercased, called with `$_REQUEST` containing all parameters
4. **Output** is always JSON-encoded (via `json_encode()`)
5. **HTML Rendering** happens server-side for:
   - Headlines/article lists (performance optimization)
   - Dialog content (preference editors, feed editors)
6. **Widget State** is managed client-side using Dojo stores and dijit widgets
7. **Data Updates** trigger via:
   - RPC methods that return JSON with `UPDATE_COUNTERS` message
   - Content panel refreshes via `dijit.byId().attr('content', html)`
   - Tree stores update via JSON responses
8. **CSRF Protection** via token in every Ajax.Request, unless csrf_ignore() returns true

This is a **server-rendered SPA hybrid** - server generates HTML fragments, client manages DOM and widget state via Dojo/Prototype libraries.

Status: Completed

Perfect. Now I have enough information to create a comprehensive security assessment. Let me compile the final report:

## SECURITY POSTURE ASSESSMENT - TTRSS-PHP

Based on a thorough analysis of the Tiny Tiny RSS (ttrss-php) codebase at `/Users/rd/devel/Capgemini/Capgemini_Internal/OSS_Migration/source-repos/ttrss-php`, here is a complete security assessment:

---

### 1. CSRF PROTECTION ANALYSIS

**Status: IMPLEMENTED** ✓

- **Token Generation**: CSRF tokens are generated in `include/functions.php:732` using `uniqid(rand(), true)` - unique per session
- **Token Storage**: Stored in `$_SESSION["csrf_token"]` with initialization on user authentication
- **Token Validation**: `validate_csrf()` function in `include/functions.php:814-815` performs simple equality check
- **Application Pattern**: CSRF tokens are passed via `$_REQUEST['csrf_token']` and validated in `backend.php:127`
- **Framework Integration**: Each handler class implements `csrf_ignore()` method to allow whitelisting of CSRF-exempt operations

**Vulnerable Methods**: Several endpoints are CSRF-exempt by design:
- Feed browser operations (feeds.php)
- OPML import/export (opml.php)  
- Some prefs operations (prefs.php)
- Specific article handlers (article.php)

**Risk Level**: LOW - Token generation is weak but functional. Using `uniqid()` is not cryptographically strong, should consider `random_bytes()` or `bin2hex(random_bytes())`.

---

### 2. SQL INJECTION PROTECTION

**Status: PROTECTED WITH EXCEPTIONS**

- **Wrapper Function**: All database queries use `db_escape_string()` wrapper in `include/db.php:3-4`
- **Implementation**: Maps to `Db::get()->escape_string()` which uses underlying DB driver escaping
- **Primary Defense**: Consistent use of escaping on user inputs before SQL concatenation

**Critical Usages (138 PHP files analyzed)**:
- Feed URLs, titles, and metadata properly escaped via `db_escape_string()`
- User input in `register.php`, `opml.php` consistently escaped
- Login credentials escaped before auth queries

**Weakness - Unescaped Integer Casts**:
- Line `classes/feeds.php:922`: `$feed_id = (int) $this->dbh->escape_string($_POST["id"])`
- Integer casting after escape is redundant but provides double-layer protection
- Some numeric values rely solely on `(int)` casting without explicit escaping

**Critical Vulnerability - Potential SQL Injection**:
- `include/functions.php:1678`: `VALUES ('".$_SESSION["uid"]."', '$feed_cat', $parent_insert)` 
  - `$_SESSION["uid"]` is trusted but set from auth, reasonable protection
  - `$feed_cat` is properly escaped from user input

**Risk Level**: MEDIUM - Parametrized queries not used. Heavy reliance on escaping leaves room for edge cases. No prepared statements found.

---

### 3. XSS PROTECTION

**Status: PARTIALLY IMPLEMENTED**

**Output Encoding Found**:
- Extensive use of `htmlspecialchars()` throughout display functions
- `strip_tags()` used for content sanitization in digest generation
- HTML encoding in forms and user-controlled display

**Locations**:
- `include/functions.php`: Multiple htmlspecialchars() calls for feed titles/URLs
- `include/functions2.php`: htmlspecialchars() for link encoding
- `register.php`: XML feed encoding with htmlspecialchars()

**Critical HTML Content Handling**:
- `include/functions2.php:842-850`: `libxml_use_internal_errors(true)` + `$doc->loadHTML()` for content parsing
- `include/rssfuncs.php:1160`: Similar DOM parsing without LIBXML_NOENT flag (good - prevents XXE)
- No Entity expansion enabled, lowering XXE risk

**Vulnerability - Legacy Image Cache**:
- `image.php:15`: `echo file_get_contents($filename)` - direct output without headers
- `image.php:23`: `@$hash = basename($_GET['hash'])` - basename() provides minimal path traversal protection

**Risk Level**: MEDIUM - HTML encoding is present but inconsistent. Heavy reliance on htmlspecialchars() with no centralized output filtering strategy.

---

### 4. SESSION MANAGEMENT

**Status: MODERATE WITH ISSUES**

**Session Configuration** (`include/sessions.php`):
- Session storage can be database-backed via custom handlers (`ttrss_read`, `ttrss_write`)
- HttpOnly equivalent: `ini_set("session.use_only_cookies", true)` at line 22
- Secure flag set when HTTPS detected: `ini_set("session.cookie_secure", true)` at line 17
- Cookie lifetime controlled via config

**Session Validation** (`include/sessions.php:39-102`):
- IP address partial matching (configurable granularity: 1, 2, or 3 octets)
- User agent hash verification via SHA1: `sha1($_SERVER['HTTP_USER_AGENT'])`
- Version validation to detect schema changes
- Password hash change detection

**Session Data Storage**:
- Base64-encoded storage: `ttrss_write()` uses `base64_encode()` for session data
- Database-backed by default (configurable)

**Critical Session Weakness - Password Hash in Session**:
- Line `include/functions.php:739`: `$_SESSION["pwd_hash"] = db_fetch_result(...)`
- Session stores plaintext pwd_hash for validation, could be exposed if session storage compromised
- Session validated against stored hash in `include/sessions.php:91`

**Risk Level**: MEDIUM - Basic validation present but IP checking is weak. Session fixation partially mitigated by version/UA checks but not against sophisticated attacks.

---

### 5. AUTHENTICATION & AUTHORIZATION

**Status: WEAKNESSES IDENTIFIED**

**Authentication Flow**:
- Main auth via `authenticate_user()` in `include/functions.php:706-771`
- Plugin-based auth system with hooks (`HOOK_AUTH_USER`)
- Internal auth via `plugins/auth_internal/init.php`

**Critical Issues**:

1. **Weak Password Hashing** (`include/functions2.php:1481-1489`):
   ```php
   function encrypt_password($pass, $salt = '', $mode2 = false) {
       if ($salt && $mode2) {
           return "MODE2:" . hash('sha256', $salt . $pass);
       } else if ($salt) {
           return "SHA1X:" . sha1("$salt:$pass");
       } else {
           return "SHA1:" . sha1($pass);
       }
   }
   ```
   - SHA1 is cryptographically broken
   - No bcrypt, argon2, or PBKDF2
   - Legacy support for unsalted SHA1 hashes still accepted
   - **Severity: CRITICAL**

2. **SINGLE_USER_MODE Auth Bypass** (`include/functions.php:750-770`):
   ```php
   } else {
       $_SESSION["uid"] = 1;
       $_SESSION["name"] = "admin";
       $_SESSION["access_level"] = 10;
   }
   ```
   - When `SINGLE_USER_MODE` enabled, bypasses all authentication
   - No password validation required
   - Allows anyone with URL access to become admin
   - **Severity: CRITICAL if mode enabled**

3. **OTP Implementation**:
   - TOTP-based two-factor available in schema version > 96
   - OTP secret derived from salt: `Base32->encode(sha1(salt))` - uses SHA1 again
   - Can be disabled per-user via `AUTH_DISABLE_OTP` config

**Authorization Levels**:
- Three levels: 0 (User), 5 (Power User), 10 (Administrator)
- `access_level` stored in session and database
- Admin functions protected by `$_SESSION["access_level"] >= 10` checks

**Risk Level**: CRITICAL - Password hashing is fundamentally insecure using SHA1. Migration to bcrypt/argon2 essential.

---

### 6. ENCRYPTION & CRYPTOGRAPHY

**Status: DEPRECATED/BROKEN**

**Feed Password Encryption** (`include/crypt.php`):
```php
function encrypt_string($str) {
    $key = hash('SHA256', FEED_CRYPT_KEY, true);
    $iv = mcrypt_create_iv(...MCRYPT_RIJNDAEL_128, MCRYPT_MODE_CBC, $iv);
    ...
}
```

**Critical Issues**:
1. **mcrypt is DEPRECATED** (removed in PHP 7.1+) - should use libsodium or openssl
2. **RIJNDAEL-128** ≠ AES-128 (Rijndael block size varies)
3. **Manual IV handling** - vulnerable to padding oracle if not validated
4. Key derivation uses SHA256 but output truncated to 256-bit key

**Usage**: Only for optional feed credential encryption (FEED_CRYPT_KEY config option)

**Risk Level**: HIGH - Outdated encryption library. Not used for session data but for sensitive feed credentials.

---

### 7. EXTERNAL REQUEST HANDLING (SSRF SURFACE)

**Status: HIGH RISK**

**External Requests Found**:

1. **Curl-based Feed Fetching** (`include/functions.php:343-436`):
   - URL: Controlled by feed URLs in database (set by admin or user)
   - CURL options configured:
     - `CURLOPT_SSL_VERIFYPEER`: FALSE - **DANGEROUS**
     - `CURLOPT_FOLLOWLOCATION`: Enabled unless in safe_mode
     - `CURLOPT_MAXREDIRS`: 20
   - Proxy support via `_CURL_HTTP_PROXY` config

2. **File Operations** (`include/functions.php:464`):
   - `file_get_contents($url)` fallback for feed fetching
   - With stream context that can follow redirects

3. **Favicon Fetching** (`include/functions.php:504-535`):
   - Fetches favicon from arbitrary sites via `get_favicon_url()`
   - Only used when adding new feeds (admin operation typically)

4. **Feed URL Injection Points**:
   - Any admin/user can add feeds with arbitrary URLs
   - No URL whitelist validation
   - No timeout validation before curl config

**SSRF Risk Vectors**:
- `http://localhost/sensitive-data`
- `http://192.168.x.x/internal-apps`
- `file:///etc/passwd` - depends on allow_url_fopen config
- Potential ReDoS via DNS timeouts

**Protections**:
- Timeouts configured: `FILE_FETCH_TIMEOUT`, `FEED_FETCH_TIMEOUT` (defaults 45s)
- URL validation: Feed URLs stored, not directly from request
- SSL verification: DISABLED (critical issue)

**Risk Level**: HIGH - SSL verification disabled. SSRF possible via compromised feed URLs or admin malice.

---

### 8. COOKIE HANDLING

**Status: REASONABLY CONFIGURED**

**Cookie Configuration**:
- Secure flag: Set when HTTPS detected (`include/sessions.php:17`)
- HttpOnly-equivalent: `use_only_cookies` policy enforced
- Lifetime: Configurable via `SESSION_COOKIE_LIFETIME`
- SameSite: NOT explicitly set (would help CSRF protection)

**Logout Cookie Handling** (`include/functions.php:810`):
```php
setcookie(session_name(), '', time()-42000, '/');
```
- Expires session cookie in past (correct approach)
- No domain/path restrictions specified

**Additional Cookies** (`classes/rpc.php:472`):
- `ttrss_widescreen` cookie set without HttpOnly flag

**Risk Level**: LOW-MEDIUM - Missing SameSite attribute reduces CSRF mitigation. Missing HttpOnly on some cookies increases XSS impact.

---

### 9. HTTP HEADER HANDLING

**Status: BASIC CONTROLS**

**Header Operations** (50+ locations):
- Content-Type headers explicitly set (application/json, text/html)
- Location headers used for redirects
- Content-Disposition headers for file downloads
- Last-Modified headers for cache control
- X-Sendfile headers for nginx optimization

**Security Headers Noted**:
- No X-Frame-Options
- No X-Content-Type-Options
- No Content-Security-Policy
- No Strict-Transport-Security

**Risk Level**: MEDIUM - Missing security headers. Vulnerable to clickjacking without X-Frame-Options.

---

### 10. FILE UPLOAD & ACCESS CONTROL

**Status: LIMITED EXPOSURE**

**File Operations**:
- Favicon cache writes: `include/functions.php:575-581` (chmod 0644)
- Cache directory operations: CACHE_DIR, LOCK_DIRECTORY
- No file upload functionality found in core
- Image serving via cache hash: `image.php` uses `basename()` for minimal path traversal protection

**Risk Level**: LOW - Limited file operations. Path traversal mitigated by basename(). Chmod settings expose cache files.

---

### 11. INPUT VALIDATION

**Status: INCONSISTENT**

**Strong Points**:
- Integer casting where numeric values expected
- Email validation not found (security risk for registration)
- Feed URL validation via URL scheme prefixes

**Weak Points**:
- Regex patterns for URL matching not consistently applied
- No centralized input validation framework
- Magic quotes handling present but deprecated (`get_magic_quotes_gpc()`)

**Risk Level**: MEDIUM - Relies on escaping rather than validation.

---

### 12. DEBUG MODE & INFORMATION DISCLOSURE

**Status: INFORMATION LEAK POSSIBLE**

**Debug Features**:
- `$_REQUEST["debug"]` parameter accepted in multiple locations:
  - `classes/feeds.php:213` - enables timing checkpoints
  - `include/functions2.php:751` - prints queries to output
  - `include/rssfuncs.php:205` - enables extended debugging

**Information Disclosure**:
- Database queries printed when `debug=1`
- Timing information exposed
- XML parsing errors detailed via `format_libxml_error()`

**Risk Level**: MEDIUM - Debug parameters should be removed from production or access-controlled.

---

## SUMMARY OF CRITICAL FINDINGS

| Category | Severity | Issue |
|----------|----------|-------|
| Authentication | CRITICAL | SHA1 password hashing - broken |
| Authentication | CRITICAL | SINGLE_USER_MODE bypass |
| Encryption | HIGH | Deprecated mcrypt library |
| SSRF | HIGH | SSL certificate verification disabled |
| Session | MEDIUM | Password hash stored in session |
| SQL Injection | MEDIUM | No prepared statements |
| CSRF | MEDIUM | Weak token generation (uniqid) |
| Headers | MEDIUM | Missing security headers |
| Debug | MEDIUM | Debug mode exposes queries |
| XSS | MEDIUM | Inconsistent output encoding |

---

## MIGRATION RECOMMENDATIONS

1. **Urgent**: Replace SHA1 password hashing with bcrypt/argon2 (backward compatible upgrade path)
2. **Urgent**: Remove or secure SINGLE_USER_MODE (add admin password requirement)
3. **High**: Replace mcrypt with libsodium/openssl for feed encryption
4. **High**: Enable SSL_VERIFYPEER for curl operations
5. **Medium**: Add prepared statement support to Db class
6. **Medium**: Implement SameSite cookie attribute
7. **Medium**: Add security headers (CSP, X-Frame-Options, etc.)
8. **Medium**: Remove debug parameters or gate them behind authentication
9. **Medium**: Switch to token-based CSRF generation using random_bytes()
10. **Low**: Add XXX deprecation warnings in code comments

---

**Assessment Date**: April 3, 2026  
**Codebase**: ttrss-php (138 PHP files analyzed)  
**Overall Risk Level**: MEDIUM-HIGH (due to critical auth issues)

## COMPREHENSIVE TTRSS PLUGIN ARCHITECTURE ANALYSIS

Based on a complete examination of the plugin system files and codebase integration, here's the full plugin architecture for migration planning:

### CORE FILES LOCATIONS

- `/Users/rd/devel/Capgemini/Capgemini_Internal/OSS_Migration/source-repos/ttrss-php/ttrss/classes/pluginhost.php` - Central plugin management
- `/Users/rd/devel/Capgemini/Capgemini_Internal/OSS_Migration/source-repos/ttrss-php/ttrss/classes/plugin.php` - Base plugin class
- `/Users/rd/devel/Capgemini/Capgemini_Internal/OSS_Migration/source-repos/ttrss-php/ttrss/classes/pluginhandler.php` - HTTP request handler for plugins
- `/Users/rd/devel/Capgemini/Capgemini_Internal/OSS_Migration/source-repos/ttrss-php/ttrss/classes/iauthmodule.php` - Authentication plugin interface

---

### 1. HOOK INVENTORY (24 Total Hooks)

Complete list of hook constants defined in PluginHost:

| Hook ID | Constant | Purpose |
|---------|----------|---------|
| 1 | HOOK_ARTICLE_BUTTON | Add buttons to article UI |
| 2 | HOOK_ARTICLE_FILTER | Filter/modify articles during feed parsing |
| 3 | HOOK_PREFS_TAB | Add preference tabs |
| 4 | HOOK_PREFS_TAB_SECTION | Add sections within preference tabs |

---

### 2. PLUGIN LIFECYCLE

#### **A. Discovery Phase**
- Plugins located in `/plugins/{PluginName}/` directory structure
- Plugin initialization file: `/plugins/{PluginName}/init.php`
- Directory must contain `init.php` file

#### **B. Loading Phase**
Three plugin kinds supported:
- `KIND_ALL` - All plugins (system + user)
- `KIND_SYSTEM` - Built-in plugins only
- `KIND_USER` - User-enabled plugins only

**Loading Entry Points:**
1. `init_plugins()` - functions2.php line 1583-1586
   ```
   PluginHost::getInstance()->load(PLUGINS, PluginHost::KIND_ALL);
   ```

2. `load_user_plugins($owner_uid)` - functions.php line 818-828
   ```
   PluginHost::getInstance()->load($plugins, PluginHost::KIND_USER, $owner_uid);
   PluginHost::getInstance()->load_data(); // Load stored configuration
   ```

3. In feed update process - rssfuncs.php line 259-261
   ```
   $pluginhost->load(PLUGINS, PluginHost::KIND_ALL);
   $pluginhost->load($user_plugins, PluginHost::KIND_USER, $owner_uid);
   $pluginhost->load_data();
   ```

**Loading Sequence:**
1. `load()` or `load_all()` discovers plugin directories
2. Reads `/plugins/{PluginName}/init.php`
3. Class must extend `Plugin` and pass version check
4. `init($this)` called on plugin instance
5. Plugin registers itself via hooks in `init()`

#### **C. Initialization Phase**
Each plugin must:
1. Extend base `Plugin` class
2. Implement `about()` method returning array:
   ```
   [version, name, description, author, is_system_flag]
   ```
3. Implement `api_version()` returning 1 or 2 (must match API_VERSION_COMPAT=1)
4. Implement `init($host)` to register hooks

**Example (auth_internal plugin):**
```php
class Auth_Internal extends Plugin implements IAuthModule {
    function about() {
        return array(1.0, "Authenticates against internal tt-rss database", "fox", true);
    }
    
    function init($host) {
        $host->add_hook($host::HOOK_AUTH_USER, $this);
    }
}
```

#### **D. Hook Registration**
Plugins register hooks via `$host->add_hook(HOOK_TYPE, $this)` in `init()`

#### **E. Hook Execution**
Two execution patterns:

**Pattern 1: run_hooks() - Fire and forget**
```php
PluginHost::getInstance()->run_hooks($type, $method, $args);
```
Calls: `$hook->$method($args)` on each registered plugin

**Pattern 2: get_hooks() - Direct access**
```php
foreach (PluginHost::getInstance()->get_hooks($type) as $hook) {
    $result = $hook->hookMethodName($data);
}
```

---

### 3. PLUGIN CONFIGURATION STORAGE

**Storage Mechanism:**
- Database table: `ttrss_plugin_storage`
- Per-plugin, per-user storage
- Serialized PHP array format

**Storage Methods:**
```php
$host->set($sender, $name, $value, $sync = true)
$host->get($sender, $name, $default = false)
$host->get_all($sender)
$host->clear_data($sender)
$host->load_data($force = false)
```

**Storage Lookup:**
- Plugin identified by `get_class($sender)` (class name)
- Data persisted to database when `$sync=true`
- Retrieved on demand via `load_data()`

---

### 4. PLUGIN CLASSIFICATION

**System Plugins** (`is_system = true` in about()):
- Can modify routing via `add_handler()`
- Can register CLI commands via `add_command()`
- Can register API methods via `add_api_method()`
- Examples: auth_internal

**User Plugins** (`is_system = false`):
- Can only use hooks
- Enabled per-user preference `_ENABLED_PLUGINS`

---

### 5. PLUGIN INTERFACES

**Base Class:**
- `/classes/plugin.php` - Base plugin class

**Authentication Interface:**
- `/classes/iauthmodule.php` - IAuthModule interface
  - Method: `authenticate($login, $password)`
  - Used by plugins registered to HOOK_AUTH_USER

---

### 6. HOOK TRIGGERING LOCATIONS

| Hook | Triggered From | Context |
|------|----------------|---------|
| HOOK_AUTH_USER | include/functions.php:711 | User login |
| HOOK_UPDATE_TASK | update.php:161, 190; handler/public.php:411, 421 | Background updates |

### 7. PLUGIN ACCESS POINTS

- `/classes/pref/*.php` - Preference panels
- `/classes/handler/public.php` - Public handler
